### [214] [Mask World Model: Predicting What Matters for Robust Robot Policy Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19683)
*Yunfan Lou,Xiaowei Chi,Xiaojie Zhang,Zezhong Qian,Chengxuan Li,Rongyu Zhang,Yaoxu Lyu,Guoyu Song,Chuyao Fu,Haoxuan Xu,Pengwei Wang,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新型的世界模型Mask World Model（MWM），通过预测语义掩码的动态变化来提升机器人泛化能力，有效过滤视觉噪音，并在多个基准测试中优于RGB视频预测方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有利用大规模视频生成训练的世界模型方法常常会过拟合于与任务无关的背景或光照变化等因素，导致机器人策略泛化能力弱、控制不可靠。为解决这一难题，作者希望从根本上提升对物理动态和关联的建模能力。

Method: 作者提出MWM，利用视频扩散架构预测语义掩码的变化而不是像素级RGB图像，这种做法强制模型关注物理结构和接触关系，并与扩散式策略头集成，实现端到端的鲁棒控制。

Result: MWM在LIBERO和RLBench基准模拟环境中远优于现有RGB视频为主的世界模型。同时，在现实机器人实验及抗干扰评测（如随机掩码剔除）中，表现出更强泛化能力和对纹理信息丢失的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 将物理语义掩码建模引入世界模型能极大提升机器人策略泛化性、鲁棒性，为通用机器人学习指明了更有前景的方向。

Abstract: World models derived from large-scale video generative pre-training have emerged as a promising paradigm for generalist robot policy learning. However, standard approaches often focus on high-fidelity RGB video prediction, this can result in overfitting to irrelevant factors, such as dynamic backgrounds and illumination changes. These distractions reduce the model's ability to generalize, ultimately leading to unreliable and fragile control policies. To address this, we introduce the Mask World Model (MWM), which leverages video diffusion architectures to predict the evolution of semantic masks instead of pixels. This shift imposes a geometric information bottleneck, forcing the model to capture essential physical dynamics and contact relations while filtering out visual noise. We seamlessly integrate this mask dynamics backbone with a diffusion-based policy head to enable robust end-to-end control. Extensive evaluations demonstrate the superiority of MWM on the LIBERO and RLBench simulation benchmarks, significantly outperforming the state-of-the-art RGB-based world models. Furthermore, real-world experiments and robustness evaluation (via random token pruning) reveal that MWM exhibits superior generalization capabilities and robust resilience to texture information loss.

</details>


### [215] [VLA Foundry: A Unified Framework for Training Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19728)
*Jean Mercat,Sedrick Keh,Kushal Arora,Isabella Huang,Paarth Shah,Haruki Nishimura,Shun Iwase,Katherine Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了VLA Foundry，一个开源框架，实现了LLM（大语言模型）、VLM（视觉语言模型）和VLA（视觉语言行动模型）在同一代码库中的统一训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前开源VLA的工作多侧重于动作训练阶段，且难以整合不同的预训练流程，造成开发障碍和效率低下。因此，作者希望通过统一框架解决训练流程割裂、操作复杂等问题。

Method: VLA Foundry提供了端到端的共享训练栈，涵盖从语言预训练到动作专家微调。支持从头训练和利用Hugging Face上现有模型骨干。作者演示了两类模型：一是完全从头训练的LLM→VLM→VLA流水线模型，二是基于预训练Qwen3-VL骨干构建的模型。同时对评估模拟器及分析工具STEP进行了易用性改进。

Result: 在开放数据模拟器LBM Eval中评估，完全从头训练的模型表现达到作者之前闭源工作的水平，而基于Qwen3-VL骨干的模型实现了高效多任务操控，显著超越了基线。

Conclusion: VLA Foundry为统一VLA相关模型训练提供了高效、开源的解决方案，支持灵活拓展与复现实验。相关代码、权重和演示均已公开，便于社区使用和推动领域发展。

Abstract: We present VLA Foundry, an open-source framework that unifies LLM, VLM, and VLA training in a single codebase. Most open-source VLA efforts specialize on the action training stage, often stitching together incompatible pretraining pipelines. VLA Foundry instead provides a shared training stack with end-to-end control, from language pretraining to action-expert fine-tuning. VLA Foundry supports both from-scratch training and pretrained backbones from Hugging Face. To demonstrate the utility of our framework, we train and release two types of models: the first trained fully from scratch through our LLM-->VLM-->VLA pipeline and the second built on the pretrained Qwen3-VL backbone. We evaluate closed-loop policy performance of both models on LBM Eval, an open-data, open-source simulator. We also contribute usability improvements to the simulator and the STEP analysis tools for easier public use. In the nominal evaluation setting, our fully-open from-scratch model is on par with our prior closed-source work and substituting in the Qwen3-VL backbone leads to a strong multi-task table top manipulation policy outperforming our baseline by a wide margin. The VLA Foundry codebase is available at https://github.com/TRI-ML/vla_foundry and all multi-task model weights are released on https://huggingface.co/collections/TRI-ML/vla-foundry. Additional qualitative videos are available on the project website https://tri-ml.github.io/vla_foundry.

</details>


### [216] [UniT: Toward a Unified Physical Language for Human-to-Humanoid Policy Learning and World Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.19734)
*Boyu Chen,Yi Chen,Lu Qiu,Jerry Bai,Yuying Ge,Yixiao Ge*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新方法UniT，利用视觉锚定实现人类到仿人机器人动作迁移，把多源异构数据转化为通用的物理意图，极大提高了数据利用率和泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仿人机器人基础模型的发展受限于机器人数据的稀缺，而大量可用的人类自我视角数据尚难有效应用于仿人机器人，主要障碍在于两者的运动学差异。论文旨在打破这一迁移壁垒，找到共享物理后果的通用编码方式。

Method: 提出了UniT框架，通过视觉锚定的三分支跨重构机制，将多模态（动作与视觉）信息提纯并融合到一个离散的、与具体形态无关的物理意图空间。具体包括：动作预测视觉（锚定物理结果）、视觉重建动作（剔除无关因素）、融合分支（生成统一Token）。

Result: 1）策略学习（VLA-UniT）：实现了高效利用多样人类数据，在仿人机器人仿真和实际环境中达到最优数据效率和极强的任务泛化能力（支持零样本迁移）。2）世界建模（WM-UniT）：通过统一Token对齐不同形态的动力学，实现人到仿人的动作直接迁移，提升了仿人视频生成的可控性。t-SNE可视化验证了人和仿人特征在共享流形上的融合。

Conclusion: UniT方法有效打通了人类与仿人机器人在感知与动作表达上的鸿沟，为大规模人类知识迁移到仿人机器人开辟了可扩展路径，有助于实现通用性更强的仿人能力。

Abstract: Scaling humanoid foundation models is bottlenecked by the scarcity of robotic data. While massive egocentric human data offers a scalable alternative, bridging the cross-embodiment chasm remains a fundamental challenge due to kinematic mismatches. We introduce UniT (Unified Latent Action Tokenizer via Visual Anchoring), a framework that establishes a unified physical language for human-to-humanoid transfer. Grounded in the philosophy that heterogeneous kinematics share universal visual consequences, UniT employs a tri-branch cross-reconstruction mechanism: actions predict vision to anchor kinematics to physical outcomes, while vision reconstructs actions to filter out irrelevant visual confounders. Concurrently, a fusion branch synergies these purified modalities into a shared discrete latent space of embodiment-agnostic physical intents. We validate UniT across two paradigms: 1) Policy Learning (VLA-UniT): By predicting these unified tokens, it effectively leverages diverse human data to achieve state-of-the-art data efficiency and robust out-of-distribution (OOD) generalization on both humanoid simulation benchmark and real-world deployments, notably demonstrating zero-shot task transfer. 2) World Modeling (WM-UniT): By aligning cross-embodiment dynamics via unified tokens as conditions, it realizes direct human-to-humanoid action transfer. This alignment ensures that human data seamlessly translates into enhanced action controllability for humanoid video generation. Ultimately, by inducing a highly aligned cross-embodiment representation (empirically verified by t-SNE visualizations revealing the convergence of human and humanoid features into a shared manifold), UniT offers a scalable path to distill vast human knowledge into general-purpose humanoid capabilities.

</details>
